I've uploaded a python code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
[Bug]: Continuous aggregates with time_bucket hourly and timezone fail to update
### What type of bug is this?

Incorrect result, Unexpected error

### What subsystems and features are affected?

Continuous aggregate

### What happened?

I have a number of Continuous aggregates that uses hourly buckets
```
 time_bucket(interval '1 hour', hypertable_name.time, 'Asia/Dubai')  AS bucket
 ```
 
 I noticed that i stopped seeing the new results after recreating the hypertable. After hours of debugging i pinned down that the hourly buckets dont refresh when used with timezone
 
 
![image](https://github.com/timescale/timescaledb/assets/42375159/6914e802-3fb7-4eb6-ad95-fcd1e0fcfaee)


### TimescaleDB version affected

2.14.2 and 2.15.0

### PostgreSQL version used

15.6

### What operating system did you use?

Arch Linux and Ubuntu Linux

### What installation method did you use?

Deb/Apt

### What platform did you run on?

On prem/Self-hosted

### Relevant log output and stack trace


### How can we reproduce the bug?

```bash
CREATE TABLE metrics (
    sensor_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    value DOUBLE PRECISION NOT NULL,
    timestamp TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL
);
SELECT create_hypertable('metrics', 'timestamp');


-- insert data into the hyper table
INSERT INTO metrics
SELECT
    s.sensor_id,
    random()*50 + 10,
    timestamp
FROM
    generate_series(DATE (now() - interval '6 month'), (now() - interval '5 day'), INTERVAL '1 hours') AS timestamp
        CROSS JOIN (SELECT generate_series(1, 200) as sensor_id) as s;


-- hourly continuous aggregate with timezone
CREATE MATERIALIZED VIEW datalake_hourly
WITH (timescaledb.continuous, timescaledb.materialized_only = true) AS
            SELECT
                time_bucket(INTERVAL '1 hour', metrics.timestamp, 'Asia/Dubai') AS bucket,
                sensor_id,
                count(*) as count_items
            FROM metrics
            GROUP BY bucket, sensor_id;
           


SELECT add_continuous_aggregate_policy(
        'datalake_hourly',
        start_offset => INTERVAL '3 months',
        end_offset => Null,
        schedule_interval => INTERVAL '15 seconds'
);        


-- insert few more rows
INSERT INTO metrics
SELECT
    s.sensor_id,
    random()*50 + 10,
    timestamp
FROM
    generate_series((now() - interval '5 day'), now(), INTERVAL '1 hour') AS timestamp
        CROSS JOIN (SELECT generate_series(1, 200) as sensor_id) as s;
        
-- wait and check the continuous aggregate
SELECT 
		timescaledb_information.jobs.job_id,
		timescaledb_information.jobs.application_name,
		timescaledb_information.jobs.initial_start,
		timescaledb_information.jobs.next_start,
		timescaledb_information.jobs.config,
		timescaledb_information.jobs.schedule_interval,
		timescaledb_information.jobs.max_runtime ,
		timescaledb_information.jobs.max_retries  ,   
		timescaledb_information.jobs.retry_period ,  
		timescaledb_information.jobs.scheduled ,
		timescaledb_information.jobs.fixed_schedule , 
		timescaledb_information.jobs.hypertable_name , 
		timescaledb_information.continuous_aggregates.view_name ,
		last_run_started_at ,
       job_status,
       last_run_status,
       last_successful_finish ,
       total_runs,
       total_failures ,
       total_successes 
FROM timescaledb_information.jobs
left join timescaledb_information.job_stats on timescaledb_information.jobs.job_id  =  timescaledb_information.job_stats.job_id 
left join timescaledb_information.continuous_aggregates on timescaledb_information.continuous_aggregates.materialization_hypertable_name  =  timescaledb_information.jobs.hypertable_name
order by job_id;
```

    59	/*
    60	 * Get the mem_guard callbacks.
    61	 *
    62	 * You might get a NULL pointer back if there are no mem_guard installed, so
    63	 * check before using.
    64	 */
    65	MGCallbacks *
    66	ts_get_mem_guard_callbacks(void)
    67	{
    68	        static MGCallbacks **mem_guard_callback_ptr = NULL;
    69	
    70	        if (mem_guard_callback_ptr)
    71	                return *mem_guard_callback_ptr;
    72	
    73	        mem_guard_callback_ptr = (MGCallbacks **) find_rendezvous_variable(MG_CALLBACKS_VAR_NAME);
    74

    84	BackgroundWorkerHandle *
    85	ts_bgw_job_start(BgwJob *job, Oid user_oid)
    86	{
    87	        BgwParams bgw_params = {
    88	                .job_id = Int32GetDatum(job->fd.id),

    95

    99	static void
   100	job_execute_function(FuncExpr *funcexpr)
   101	{
   102	        bool isnull;
   103	
   104	        EState *estate = CreateExecutorState();
   105	        ExprContext *econtext = CreateExprContext(estate);
   106	
   107	        ExprState *es = ExecPrepareExpr((Expr *) funcexpr, estate);
   108	        ExecEvalExpr(es, econtext, &isnull);
   109	        FreeExprContext(econtext, true);
   110	        FreeExecutorState(estate);
   111	}
   112	
   113	/**
   114	 * Run configuration check validation function.
   115	 *
   116	 * This will run the configuration check validation function registered for
   117	 * the job. If a new job is added, the job_id is going to be zero.
   118	 */
   119	void
   120	ts_bgw_job_run_config_check(Oid check, int32 job_id, Jsonb *config)
   121	{
   122	        /* Nothing to check if there is no check function provided */
   123	        if (!OidIsValid(check))
   124	                return;
   125	
   126	        /* NULL config may be valid */
   127	        Const *arg;
   128	        if (config == NULL)
   129	                arg = makeNullConst(JSONBOID, -1, InvalidOid);
   130	        else
   131	                arg = makeConst(JSONBOID, -1, InvalidOid, -1, JsonbPGetDatum(config), false, false);
   132	
   133	        List *args = list_make1(arg);
   134	        FuncExpr *funcexpr =
   135	                makeFuncExpr(check, VOIDOID, args, InvalidOid, InvalidOid, COERCE_EXPLICIT_CALL);
   136	
   137	        if (get_func_prokind(check) == PROKIND_FUNCTION)
   138	                job_execute_function(funcexpr);
   139	        else
   140	                ereport(ERROR,
   141	                                (errcode(ERRCODE_FEATURE_NOT_SUPPORTED),
   142	                                 errmsg("unsupported function type"),
   143	                                 errdetail("Only functions are allowed as custom configuration checks"),
   144	                                 errhint("Use a FUNCTION instead")));
   145	}
   146	
   147	/* Run the check function on a configuration. It will generate errors if there
   148	 * is anything wrong with the configuration, otherwise just return. If the
   149	 * check function does not exist, no checking will be done.*/
   150	static void
   151	job_config_check(BgwJob *job, Jsonb *config)
   152	{
   153	        Oid proc;
   154	        List *funcname;
   155	
   156	        /* Both should either be empty or contain a schema and name */
   157	        Assert((strlen(NameStr(job->fd.check_schema)) == 0) ==
   158	                   (strlen(NameStr(job->fd.check_schema)) == 0));
   159	
   160	        /* If there is no function, just return */
   161	        if (strlen(NameStr(job->fd.check_name)) == 0)
   162	                return;
   163	
   164	        funcname = list_make2(makeString(NameStr(job->fd.check_schema)),
   165	                                                  makeString(NameStr(job->fd.check_name)));
   166	
   167	        Oid argtypes[] = { JSONBOID };
   168	        /* Only functions allowed as custom checks, as procedures can cause errors with COMMIT
   169	         * statements */
   170	        proc = LookupFuncName(funcname, 1, argtypes, true);
   171	
   172	        /* a check function has been registered but it can't be found anymore
   173	         because it was dropped or renamed. Allow alter_job to run if that's the case
   174	         without validating the config but also print a warning */
   175	        if (OidIsValid(proc))
   176	                ts_bgw_job_run_config_check(proc, job->fd.id, config);
   177	        else
   178	                elog(WARNING,
   179	                         "function %s.%s(config jsonb) not found, skipping config validation for "
   180	                         "job %d",
   181	                         NameStr(job->fd.check_schema),
   182	                         NameStr(job->fd.check_name),
   183	                         job->fd.id);
   184	}
   185	
   186	static BgwJob *
   187	bgw_job_from_tupleinfo(TupleInfo *ti, size_t alloc_size)
   188	{
   189	        BgwJob *job;
   190	        bool should_free;
   191	        HeapTuple tuple;
   192	        MemoryContext old_ctx;
   193	        Datum values[Natts_bgw_job] = { 0 };
   194	        bool nulls[Natts_bgw_job] = { false };
   195	
   196	        /*
   197	         * allow for embedding with arbitrary alloc_size, which means we can't use
   198	         * the STRUCT_FROM_TUPLE macro
   199	         */
   200	        Assert(alloc_size >= sizeof(BgwJob));
   201	        job = MemoryContextAllocZero(ti->mctx, alloc_size);
   202	        tuple = ts_scanner_fetch_heap_tuple(ti, false, &should_free);
   203	
   204	        old_ctx = MemoryContextSwitchTo(ti->mctx);
   205	
   206	        /*
   207	         * Using heap_deform_tuple instead of GETSTRUCT since the tuple can
   208	         * contain NULL values. Some of these cannot really be null, but we check
   209	         * anyway since it is cheap and will avoid problems in the future. Note
   210	         * that the job structure is zeroed, so we only need to update the field
   211	         * if it is non-NULL.
   212	         */
   213	        heap_deform_tuple(tuple, ts_scanner_get_tupledesc(ti), values, nulls);
   214	
   215	        if (!nulls[AttrNumberGetAttrOffset(Anum_bgw_job_id)])
   216	                job->fd.id = DatumGetInt32(values[AttrNumberGetAttrOffset(Anum_bgw_job_id)]);

   233	                job->fd.fixed_schedule =
   234	                        DatumGetBool(values[AttrNumberGetAttrOffset(Anum_bgw_job_fixed_schedule)]);
   235	
   236	        if (!nulls[AttrNumberGetAttrOffset(Anum_bgw_job_initial_start)])
   237	        {

   239	                        DatumGetTimestampTz(values[AttrNumberGetAttrOffset(Anum_bgw_job_initial_start)]);

   249	                job->fd.retry_period =

   251

   253	                namestrcpy(&job->fd.proc_schema,
   254	                                   DatumGetCString(values[AttrNumberGetAttrOffset(Anum_bgw_job_proc_schema)]));
   255	        if (!nulls[AttrNumberGetAttrOffset(Anum_bgw_job_proc_name)])

   257	                                   DatumGetCString(values[AttrNumberGetAttrOffset(Anum_bgw_job_proc_name)]));
   258	        if (!nulls[AttrNumberGetAttrOffset(Anum_bgw_job_check_schema)])
   259	                namestrcpy(&job->fd.check_schema,
   260	                                   DatumGetCString(values[AttrNumberGetAttrOffset(Anum_bgw_job_check_schema)]));
   261	        if (!nulls[AttrNumberGetAttrOffset(Anum_bgw_job_check_name)])
   262	                namestrcpy(&job->fd.check_name,
   263	                                   DatumGetCString(values[AttrNumberGetAttrOffset(Anum_bgw_job_check_name)]));
   264	        if (!nulls[AttrNumberGetAttrOffset(Anum_bgw_job_owner)])
   265	                job->fd.owner = DatumGetObjectId(values[AttrNumberGetAttrOffset(Anum_bgw_job_owner)]);
   266	
   267	        if (!nulls[AttrNumberGetAttrOffset(Anum_bgw_job_scheduled)])
   268	                job->fd.scheduled = DatumGetBool(values[AttrNumberGetAttrOffset(Anum_bgw_job_scheduled)]);
   269	
   270	        if (!nulls[AttrNumberGetAttrOffset(Anum_bgw_job_hypertable_id)])
   271	                job->fd.hypertable_id =

   273	
   274	        if (!nulls[AttrNumberGetAttrOffset(Anum_bgw_job_config)])
   275	                job->fd.config = DatumGetJsonbPCopy(values[AttrNumberGetAttrOffset(Anum_bgw_job_config)]);
   276	
   277	        MemoryContextSwitchTo(old_ctx);
   278	
   279	        if (should_free)
   280	                heap_freetuple(tuple);
   281	
   282	        return job;
   283	}
   284	
   285	typedef struct AccumData
   286	{
   287	        List *list;
   288	        size_t alloc_size;
   289	} AccumData;
   290	
   291	static ScanTupleResult
   292	bgw_job_accum_tuple_found(TupleInfo *ti, void *data)
   293	{
   294	        AccumData *list_data = data;
   295	        BgwJob *job = bgw_job_from_tupleinfo(ti, list_data->alloc_size);
   296	        MemoryContext orig = MemoryContextSwitchTo(ti->mctx);
   297	
   298	        list_data->list = lappend(list_data->list, job);
   299	
   300	        MemoryContextSwitchTo(orig);
   301	        return SCAN_CONTINUE;
   302	}
   303	
   304	static ScanFilterResult
   305	bgw_job_filter_scheduled(const TupleInfo *ti, void *data)
   306	{
   307	        bool isnull;
   308	        Datum scheduled = slot_getattr(ti->slot, Anum_bgw_job_scheduled, &isnull);
   309	        Ensure(!isnull, "scheduled column was null");
   310	
   311	        return DatumGetBool(scheduled);
   312	}
   313	
   314	/* This function is meant to be used by the scheduler only
   315	 * it does not include the config field which saves us from
   316	 * detoasting and makes memory management in the scheduler
   317	 * simpler as otherwise the config field would have to be
   318	 * freed separately when freeing jobs which would prevent
   319	 * the use of list_free_deep.
   320	 * The scheduler does not need the config field only the
   321	 * individual jobs do.
   322	 * The scheduler requires jobs to be sorted by id
   323	 * which is guaranteed by the index scan on the primary key
   324	 */
   325	List *
   326	ts_bgw_job_get_scheduled(size_t alloc_size, MemoryContext mctx)
   327	{
   328	        MemoryContext old_ctx;
   329	        List *jobs = NIL;
   330	        ScanIterator iterator = ts_scan_iterator_create(BGW_JOB, AccessShareLock, mctx);
   331	
   332	        iterator.ctx.index = catalog_get_index(ts_catalog_get(), BGW_JOB, BGW_JOB_PKEY_IDX);
   333	        iterator.ctx.filter = bgw_job_filter_scheduled;
   334	
   335	        ts_scanner_foreach(&iterator)
   336	        {
   337	                TupleInfo *ti = ts_scan_iterator_tuple_info(&iterator);
   338	                bool should_free, isnull, initial_start_isnull, timezone_isnull;
   339	                Datum value, initial_start, timezone;
   340	
   341	                BgwJob *job = MemoryContextAllocZero(mctx, alloc_size);
   342	                HeapTuple tuple = ts_scanner_fetch_heap_tuple(ti, false, &should_free);
   343	
   344	                /*
   345	                 * Note that the nullable columns might have variable width, so we
   346	                 * handle them below. We can only use memcpy for the non-nullable fixed
   347	                 * width starting part of the BgwJob struct.
   348	                 */
   349	                memcpy(job, GETSTRUCT(tuple), offsetof(FormData_bgw_job, initial_start));
   350	
   351	                if (should_free)
   352	                        heap_freetuple(tuple);
   353	
   354	#ifdef USE_TELEMETRY
   355	                /* ignore telemetry jobs if telemetry is disabled */
   356	                if (!ts_telemetry_on() && ts_is_telemetry_job(job))
   357	                {
   358	                        pfree(job);
   359	                        continue;
   360	                }
   361	#endif
   362	                /* handle NULL columns */
   363	                initial_start = slot_getattr(ti->slot, Anum_bgw_job_initial_start, &initial_start_isnull);
   364	                if (!initial_start_isnull)
   365	                        job->fd.initial_start = DatumGetTimestampTz(initial_start);
   366	                else
   367	                        job->fd.initial_start = DT_NOBEGIN;
   368	
   369	                value = slot_getattr(ti->slot, Anum_bgw_job_hypertable_id, &isnull);
   370	                job->fd.hypertable_id = isnull ? 0 : DatumGetInt32(value);
   371	
   372	                /* We skip config, check_name, and check_schema since the scheduler
   373	                 * doesn't need these, it saves us from detoasting, and simplifies
   374	                 * freeing job lists in the scheduler as otherwise the config field
   375	                 * would have to be freed separately when freeing a job. */
   376	                job->fd.config = NULL;
   377	
   378	                old_ctx = MemoryContextSwitchTo(mctx);
   379	
   380	                timezone = slot_getattr(ti->slot, Anum_bgw_job_timezone, &timezone_isnull);
   381	                if (!timezone_isnull)
   382	                {
   383	                        /* We use DatumGetTextPCopy to move the detoasted value into our memory context */
   384	                        job->fd.timezone = DatumGetTextPCopy(timezone);
   385	                }
   386	                else
   387	                {
   388	                        job->fd.timezone = NULL;
   389	                }
   390	
   391	                jobs = lappend(jobs, job);
   392	                MemoryContextSwitchTo(old_ctx);
   393	        }
   394	
   395	        return jobs;
   396	}
   397	
   398	List *
   399	ts_bgw_job_get_all(size_t alloc_size, MemoryContext mctx)
   400	{
   401	        Catalog *catalog = ts_catalog_get();
   402	        AccumData list_data = {
   403	                .list = NIL,
   404	                .alloc_size = sizeof(BgwJob),
   405	        };
   406	        ScannerCtx scanctx = {
   407	                .table = catalog_get_table_id(catalog, BGW_JOB),
   408	                .data = &list_data,
   409	                .tuple_found = bgw_job_accum_tuple_found,
   410	                .lockmode = AccessShareLock,
   411	                .result_mctx = mctx,
   412	                .scandirection = ForwardScanDirection,
   413	        };
   414	
   415	        ts_scanner_scan(&scanctx);
   416	        return list_data.list;
   417	}
   418	
   419	static void
   420	init_scan_by_proc_name(ScanKeyData *scankey, const char *proc_name)
   421	{
   422	        ScanKeyInit(scankey,
   423	                                Anum_bgw_job_proc_hypertable_id_idx_proc_name,
   424	                                BTEqualStrategyNumber,
   425	                                F_NAMEEQ,
   426	                                CStringGetDatum(proc_name));
   427	}
   428	
   429	static void
   430	init_scan_by_proc_schema(ScanKeyData *scankey, const char *proc_schema)
   431	{
   432	        ScanKeyInit(scankey,
   433	                                Anum_bgw_job_proc_hypertable_id_idx_proc_schema,
   434	                                BTEqualStrategyNumber,
   435	                                F_NAMEEQ,
   436	                                CStringGetDatum(proc_schema));
   437	}
   438	
   439	static void
   440	init_scan_by_hypertable_id(ScanKeyData *scankey, int32 hypertable_id)
   441	{
   442	        ScanKeyInit(scankey,
   443	                                Anum_bgw_job_proc_hypertable_id_idx_hypertable_id,
   444	                                BTEqualStrategyNumber,
   445	                                F_INT4EQ,
   446	                                Int32GetDatum(hypertable_id));
   447	}
   448	
   449	List *
   450	ts_bgw_job_find_by_proc_and_hypertable_id(const char *proc_name, const char *proc_schema,
   451	                                                                                  int32 hypertable_id)
   452	{
   453	        Catalog *catalog = ts_catalog_get();
   454	        ScanKeyData scankey[3];
   455	        AccumData list_data = {
   456	                .list = NIL,
   457	                .alloc_size = sizeof(BgwJob),
   458	        };
   459	        ScannerCtx scanctx = {
   460	                .table = catalog_get_table_id(catalog, BGW_JOB),
   461	                .index = catalog_get_index(ts_catalog_get(), BGW_JOB, BGW_JOB_PROC_HYPERTABLE_ID_IDX),
   462	                .data = &list_data,
   463	                .scankey = scankey,
   464	                .nkeys = sizeof(scankey) / sizeof(*scankey),
   465	                .tuple_found = bgw_job_accum_tuple_found,
   466	                .lockmode = AccessShareLock,
   467	                .scandirection = ForwardScanDirection,
   468	        };
   469	
   470	        init_scan_by_proc_schema(&scankey[0], proc_schema);
   471	        init_scan_by_proc_name(&scankey[1], proc_name);
   472	        init_scan_by_hypertable_id(&scankey[2], hypertable_id);
   473	
   474	        ts_scanner_scan(&scanctx);
   475	        return list_data.list;
   476	}
   477	
   478	List *
   479	ts_bgw_job_find_by_hypertable_id(int32 hypertable_id)
   480	{
   481	        Catalog *catalog = ts_catalog_get();
   482	        ScanKeyData scankey[1];
   483	        AccumData list_data = {
   484	                .list = NIL,
   485	                .alloc_size = sizeof(BgwJob),
   486	        };
   487	        ScannerCtx scanctx = {
   488	                .table = catalog_get_table_id(catalog, BGW_JOB),
   489	                .index = catalog_get_index(ts_catalog_get(), BGW_JOB, BGW_JOB_PROC_HYPERTABLE_ID_IDX),
   490	                .data = &list_data,
   491	                .scankey = scankey,
   492	                .nkeys = sizeof(scankey) / sizeof(*scankey),
   493	                .tuple_found = bgw_job_accum_tuple_found,
   494	                .lockmode = AccessShareLock,
   495	                .scandirection = ForwardScanDirection,
   496	        };
   497	
   498	        init_scan_by_hypertable_id(&scankey[0], hypertable_id);
   499	
   500	        ts_scanner_scan(&scanctx);
   501	        return list_data.list;
   502	}
   503	
   504	static void
   505	init_scan_by_job_id(ScanIterator *iterator, int32 job_id)
   506	{
   507	        iterator->ctx.index = catalog_get_index(ts_catalog_get(), BGW_JOB, BGW_JOB_PKEY_IDX);
   508	        ts_scan_iterator_scan_key_init(iterator,
   509	                                                                   Anum_bgw_job_pkey_idx_id,
   510	                                                                   BTEqualStrategyNumber,
   511	                                                                   F_INT4EQ,
   512	                                                                   Int32GetDatum(job_id));
   513	}

    86	/*
    87	 * Get all hypertables that are using WAL-invalidations.
    88	 */
    89	static List *
    90	get_all_wal_using_hypertables(void)
    91	{
    92	        ScanIterator iterator =
    93	                ts_scan_iterator_create(CONTINUOUS_AGG, AccessShareLock, CurrentMemoryContext);
    94	        List *hypertables = NIL;
    95	
    96	        /* Collect OID of all tables using continuous aggregates */
    97	        ts_scanner_foreach(&iterator)
    98	        {
    99	                bool isnull;
   100	                Datum datum = slot_getattr(ts_scan_iterator_slot(&iterator),
   101	                                                                   Anum_continuous_agg_raw_hypertable_id,
   102	                                                                   &isnull);
   103	
   104	                Assert(!isnull);
   105	                int32 hypertable_id = DatumGetInt32(datum);
   106	                Oid relid = ts_hypertable_id_to_relid(hypertable_id, false);
   107	                if (!has_invalidation_trigger(relid))
   108	                        hypertables = list_append_unique_int(hypertables, hypertable_id);
   109	        }
   110	        ts_scan_iterator_close(&iterator);
   111	
   112	        return hypertables;
   113	}
   114	
   115	static Hypertable *
   116	cagg_get_hypertable_or_fail(int32 hypertable_id)
   117	{
   118	        Hypertable *ht = ts_hypertable_get_by_id(hypertable_id);
   119	
   120	        if (NULL == ht)
   121	                ereport(ERROR,
   122	                                (errcode(ERRCODE_INTERNAL_ERROR),
   123	                                 errmsg("invalid continuous aggregate state"),
   124	                                 errdetail("A continuous aggregate references a hypertable that does not exist.")));
   125	
   126	        return ht;
   127	}
   128	
   129	/*
   130	 * Compute the largest possible bucketed window given the time type and
   131	 * internal restrictions.
   132	 *
   133	 * The largest bucketed window is governed by restrictions set by the type and
   134	 * internal, TimescaleDB-specific legacy details (see get_max_window above for
   135	 * further explanation).
   136	 */
   137	static InternalTimeRange
   138	get_largest_bucketed_window(Oid timetype, int64 bucket_width)
   139	{
   140	        InternalTimeRange maxwindow = {
   141	                .type = timetype,
   142	                .start = ts_time_get_min(timetype),
   143	                .end = ts_time_get_end_or_max(timetype),
   144	        };
   145	        InternalTimeRange maxbuckets = {
   146	                .type = timetype,
   147	        };
   148	
   149	        /* For the MIN value, the corresponding bucket either falls on the exact
   150	         * MIN or it will be below it. Therefore, we add (bucket_width - 1) to
   151	         * move to the next bucket to be within the allowed range. */
   152	        maxwindow.start = ts_time_saturating_add(maxwindow.start, bucket_width - 1, timetype);
   153	        maxbuckets.start = ts_time_bucket_by_type(bucket_width, maxwindow.start, timetype);
   154	        maxbuckets.end = ts_time_get_end_or_max(timetype);
   155	
   156	        return maxbuckets;
   157	}
   158	
   159	/*
   160	 * Adjust the refresh window to align with inscribed buckets, so it includes buckets, which are
   161	 * fully covered by the refresh window.
   162	 *
   163	 * Bucketing refresh window is necessary for a continuous aggregate refresh, which can refresh only
   164	 * entire buckets. The result of the function is a bucketed window, where its start is at the start
   165	 * of the first bucket, which is  fully inside the refresh window, and its end is at the end of the
   166	 * last fully covered bucket.
   167	 *
   168	 * Example1, the window needs to shrink:
   169	 *    [---------)      - given refresh window
   170	 * .|....|....|....|.  - buckets
   171	 *       [----)        - inscribed bucketed window
   172	 *
   173	 * Example2, the window is already aligned:
   174	 *       [----)        - given refresh window
   175	 * .|....|....|....|.  - buckets
   176	 *       [----)        - inscribed bucketed window
   177	 *
   178	 * This function is called for the continuous aggregate policy and manual refresh. In such case
   179	 * excluding buckets, which are not fully covered by the refresh window, avoids refreshing a bucket,
   180	 * where part of its data were dropped by a retention policy. See #2198 for details.
   181	 */
   182	static InternalTimeRange
   183	compute_inscribed_bucketed_refresh_window(const ContinuousAgg *cagg,
   184	                                                                                  const InternalTimeRange *const refresh_window,
   185	                                                                                  const int64 bucket_width)
   186	{
   187	        Assert(cagg != NULL);
   188	        Assert(cagg->bucket_function != NULL);
   189	
   190	        NullableDatum NULL_DATUM = INIT_NULL_DATUM;
   191	        InternalTimeRange result = *refresh_window;
   192	        InternalTimeRange largest_bucketed_window =
   193	                get_largest_bucketed_window(refresh_window->type, bucket_width);
   194	
   195	        if (refresh_window->start <= largest_bucketed_window.start)
   196	        {
   197	                result.start = largest_bucketed_window.start;
   198	        }
   199	        else
   200	        {
   201	                /* The start time needs to be aligned with the first fully enclosed bucket.
   202	                 * So the original window start is moved to next bucket, except if the start is
   203	                 * already aligned with a bucket, thus 1 is subtracted to avoid moving into next
   204	                 * bucket in the aligned case. */
   205	                int64 included_bucket =
   206	                        ts_time_saturating_add(refresh_window->start, bucket_width - 1, refresh_window->type);
   207	                /* Get the start of the included bucket. */
   208	                result.start = ts_time_bucket_by_type_extended(bucket_width,
   209	                                                                                                           included_bucket,
   210	                                                                                                           refresh_window->type,
   211	                                                                                                           NULL_DATUM,
   212	                                                                                                           NULL_DATUM);
   213	        }
   214	
   215	        if (refresh_window->end >= largest_bucketed_window.end)
   216	        {
   217	                result.end = largest_bucketed_window.end;
   218	        }
   219	        else
   220	        {
   221	                /* The window is reduced to the beginning of the bucket, which contains the exclusive
   222	                 * end of the refresh window. */
   223	                result.end = ts_time_bucket_by_type_extended(bucket_width,
   224	                                                                                                         refresh_window->end,
   225	                                                                                                         refresh_window->type,
   226	                                                                                                         NULL_DATUM,
   227	                                                                                                         NULL_DATUM);
   228	        }
   229	        return result;
   230	}
   231	
   232	/*
   233	 * Get the offset as Datum value of an integer based bucket
   234	 */
   235	static Datum
   236	int_bucket_offset_to_datum(Oid type, const ContinuousAggBucketFunction *bucket_function)
   237	{
   238	        Assert(bucket_function->bucket_time_based == false);
   239	
   240	        switch (type)
   241	        {
   242	                case INT2OID:
   243	                        return Int16GetDatum(bucket_function->bucket_integer_offset);
   244	                case INT4OID:
   245	                        return Int32GetDatum(bucket_function->bucket_integer_offset);
   246	                case INT8OID:
   247	                        return Int64GetDatum(bucket_function->bucket_integer_offset);
   248	                default:
   249	                        elog(ERROR, "invalid integer time_bucket type \"%s\"", format_type_be(type));
   250	                        pg_unreachable();
   251	        }
   252	}
   253	
   254	/*
   255	 * Get a NullableDatum for offset and origin based on the CAgg information
   256	 */
   257	static void
   258	fill_bucket_offset_origin(const ContinuousAgg *cagg, const InternalTimeRange *const refresh_window,
   259	                                                  NullableDatum *offset, NullableDatum *origin)
   260	{
   261	        Assert(cagg != NULL);
   262	        Assert(offset != NULL);
   263	        Assert(origin != NULL);
   264	        Assert(offset->isnull);
   265	        Assert(origin->isnull);
   266	
   267	        if (cagg->bucket_function->bucket_time_based)
   268	        {
   269	                if (cagg->bucket_function->bucket_time_offset != NULL)
   270	                {
   271	                        offset->isnull = false;
   272	                        offset->value = IntervalPGetDatum(cagg->bucket_function->bucket_time_offset);
   273	                }
   274	
   275	                if (TIMESTAMP_NOT_FINITE(cagg->bucket_function->bucket_time_origin) == false)
   276	                {
   277	                        origin->isnull = false;
   278	                        if (refresh_window->type == DATEOID)
   279	                        {
   280	                                /* Date was converted into a timestamp in process_additional_timebucket_parameter(),
   281	                                 * build a Date again */
   282	                                origin->value = DirectFunctionCall1(timestamp_date,
   283	                                                                                                        TimestampGetDatum(
   284	                                                                                                                cagg->bucket_function->bucket_time_origin));
   285	                        }
   286	                        else
   287	                        {
   288	                                origin->value = TimestampGetDatum(cagg->bucket_function->bucket_time_origin);
   289	                        }
   290	                }
   291	        }
   292	        else
   293	        {
   294	                if (cagg->bucket_function->bucket_integer_offset != 0)
   295	                {
   296	                        offset->isnull = false;
   297	                        offset->value = int_bucket_offset_to_datum(refresh_window->type, cagg->bucket_function);
   298	                }
   299	        }
   300	}
   301	
   302	/*
   303	 * Adjust the refresh window to align with circumscribed buckets, so it includes buckets, which
   304	 * fully cover the refresh window.
   305	 *
   306	 * Bucketing refresh window is necessary for a continuous aggregate refresh, which can refresh only
   307	 * entire buckets. The result of the function is a bucketed window, where its start is at the start
   308	 * of a bucket, which contains the start of the refresh window, and its end is at the end of a
   309	 * bucket, which contains the end of the refresh window.
   310	 *
   311	 * Example1, the window needs to expand:
   312	 *    [---------)      - given refresh window
   313	 * .|....|....|....|.  - buckets
   314	 *  [--------------)   - circumscribed bucketed window
   315	 *
   316	 * Example2, the window is already aligned:
   317	 *       [----)        - given refresh window
   318	 * .|....|....|....|.  - buckets
   319	 *       [----)        - inscribed bucketed window
   320	 *
   321	 * This function is called for an invalidation window before refreshing it and after the
   322	 * invalidation window was adjusted to be fully inside a refresh window. In the case of a
   323	 * continuous aggregate policy or manual refresh, the refresh window is the inscribed bucketed
   324	 * window.
   325	 *
   326	 * The circumscribed behaviour is also used for a refresh on drop, when the refresh is called during
   327	 * dropping chunks manually or as part of retention policy.
   328	 */
   329	InternalTimeRange
   330	compute_circumscribed_bucketed_refresh_window(const ContinuousAgg *cagg,
   331	                                                                                          const InternalTimeRange *const refresh_window,
   332	                                                                                          const ContinuousAggBucketFunction *bucket_function)
   333	{
   334	        Assert(cagg != NULL);
   335	        Assert(cagg->bucket_function != NULL);
   336	
   337	        if (bucket_function->bucket_fixed_interval == false)
   338	        {
   339	                InternalTimeRange result = *refresh_window;
   340	                ts_compute_circumscribed_bucketed_refresh_window_variable(&result.start,
   341	                                                                                                                                  &result.end,
   342	                                                                                                                                  bucket_function);
   343	                return result;
   344	        }
   345	
   346	        /* Interval is fixed */
   347	        int64 bucket_width = ts_continuous_agg_fixed_bucket_width(bucket_function);
   348	        Assert(bucket_width > 0);
   349	
   350	        InternalTimeRange result = *refresh_window;
   351	        InternalTimeRange largest_bucketed_window =
   352	                get_largest_bucketed_window(refresh_window->type, bucket_width);
   353	
   354	        /* Get offset and origin for bucket function */
   355	        NullableDatum offset = INIT_NULL_DATUM;
   356	        NullableDatum origin = INIT_NULL_DATUM;
   357	        fill_bucket_offset_origin(cagg, refresh_window, &offset, &origin);
   358	
   359	        /* Defined offset and origin in one function is not supported */
   360	        Assert(offset.isnull == true || origin.isnull == true);
   361	
   362	        if (refresh_window->start <= largest_bucketed_window.start)
   363	        {
   364	                result.start = largest_bucketed_window.start;
   365	        }
   366	        else
   367	        {
   368	                /* For alignment with a bucket, which includes the start of the refresh window, we just
   369	                 * need to get start of the bucket. */
   370	                result.start = ts_time_bucket_by_type_extended(bucket_width,
   371	                                                                                                           refresh_window->start,
   372	                                                                                                           refresh_window->type,
   373	                                                                                                           offset,
   374	                                                                                                           origin);
   375	        }
   376	
   377	        if (refresh_window->end >= largest_bucketed_window.end)
   378	        {
   379	                result.end = largest_bucketed_window.end;
   380	        }
   381	        else
   382	        {
   383	                int64 exclusive_end;
   384	                int64 bucketed_end;
   385	
   386	                Assert(refresh_window->end > result.start);
   387	
   388	                /* The end of the window is non-inclusive so subtract one before
   389	                 * bucketing in case we're already at the end of the bucket (we don't
   390	                 * want to add an extra bucket).  */
   391	                exclusive_end = ts_time_saturating_sub(refresh_window->end, 1, refresh_window->type);
   392	                bucketed_end = ts_time_bucket_by_type_extended(bucket_width,
   393	                                                                                                           exclusive_end,
   394	                                                                                                           refresh_window->type,
   395	                                                                                                           offset,
   396	                                                                                                           origin);
   397	
   398	                /* We get the time value for the start of the bucket, so need to add
   399	                 * bucket_width to get the end of it. */
   400	                result.end = ts_time_saturating_add(bucketed_end, bucket_width, refresh_window->type);
   401	        }
   402	        return result;
   403	}
   404	
   405	/*
   406	 * Initialize the refresh state for a continuous aggregate.
   407	 *
   408	 * The state holds information for executing a refresh of a continuous aggregate.
   409	 */
   410	static void
   411	continuous_agg_refresh_init(ContinuousAggRefreshState *refresh, const ContinuousAgg *cagg,
   412	                                                        const InternalTimeRange *refresh_window)
   413	{
   414	        MemSet(refresh, 0, sizeof(*refresh));
   415	        refresh->cagg = *cagg;
   416	        refresh->cagg_ht = cagg_get_hypertable_or_fail(cagg->data.mat_hypertable_id);
   417	        refresh->refresh_window = *refresh_window;
   418	        refresh->partial_view.schema = &refresh->cagg.data.partial_view_schema;
   419	        refresh->partial_view.name = &refresh->cagg.data.partial_view_name;
   420	}
   421	
   422	/*
   423	 * Execute a refresh.
   424	 *
   425	 * The refresh will materialize the area given by the refresh window in the
   426	 * refresh state.
   427	 */
   428	static void
   429	continuous_agg_refresh_execute(const ContinuousAggRefreshState *refresh,
   430	                                                           const InternalTimeRange *bucketed_refresh_window,
   431	                                                           const int32 chunk_id)
   432	{
   433	        SchemaAndName cagg_hypertable_name = {
   434	                .schema = &refresh->cagg_ht->fd.schema_name,
   435	                .name = &refresh->cagg_ht->fd.table_name,
   436	        };
   437	        const Dimension *time_dim = hyperspace_get_open_dimension(refresh->cagg_ht->space, 0);
   438	
   439	        Assert(time_dim != NULL);
   440	
   441	        continuous_agg_update_materialization(refresh->cagg_ht,
   442	                                                                                  &refresh->cagg,
   443	                                                                                  refresh->partial_view,
   444	                                                                                  cagg_hypertable_name,
   445	                                                                                  &time_dim->fd.column_name,
   446	                                                                                  *bucketed_refresh_window,
   447	                                                                                  chunk_id);
   448	}

    18	#define TIME_BUCKET(period, timestamp, offset, min, max, result)                                   \
    19	        do                                                                                             \
    20	        {                                                                                              \
    21	                if ((period) <= 0)                                                                         \
    22	                        ereport(ERROR,                                                                         \
    23	                                        (errcode(ERRCODE_INVALID_PARAMETER_VALUE),                                     \
    24	                                         errmsg("period must be greater than 0")));                                    \
    25	                if ((offset) != 0)                                                                         \
    26	                {                                                                                          \
    27	                        /* We need to ensure that the timestamp is in range _after_ the */                     \
    28	                        /* offset is applied: when the offset is positive we need to make */                   \
    29	                        /* sure the resultant time is at least min, and when negative that */                  \
    30	                        /* it is less than the max. */                                                         \
    31	                        (offset) = (offset) % (period);                                                        \
    32	                        if (((offset) > 0 && (timestamp) < (min) + (offset)) ||                                \
    33	                                ((offset) < 0 && (timestamp) > (max) + (offset)))                                  \
    34	                                ereport(ERROR,                                                                     \
    35	                                                (errcode(ERRCODE_NUMERIC_VALUE_OUT_OF_RANGE),                              \
    36	                                                 errmsg("timestamp out of range")));                                       \
    37	                        (timestamp) -= (offset);                                                               \
    38	                }                                                                                          \
    39	                (result) = ((timestamp) / (period)) * (period);                                            \
    40	                if ((timestamp) < 0 && (timestamp) % (period))                                             \
    41	                {                                                                                          \
    42	                        if ((result) < (min) + (period))                                                       \
    43	                                ereport(ERROR,                                                                     \
    44	                                                (errcode(ERRCODE_NUMERIC_VALUE_OUT_OF_RANGE),                              \
    45	                                                 errmsg("timestamp out of range")));                                       \
    46	                        else                                                                                   \
    47	                                (result) = (result) - (period);                                                    \
    48	                }                                                                                          \
    49	                (result) += (offset);                                                                      \
    50	        } while (0)
    51

    94	#define JAN_3_2000 (2 * USECS_PER_DAY)
    95	
    96	/*
    97	 * The default origin is Monday 2000-01-03. We don't use PG epoch since it starts on a saturday.
    98	 * This makes time-buckets by a week more intuitive and aligns it with date_trunc. Since month
    99	 * bucketing ignores the day component this makes origin for month buckets 2000-01-01.
   100	 */
   101	#define DEFAULT_ORIGIN (JAN_3_2000)
   102	#define TIME_BUCKET_TS(period, timestamp, result, shift)                                           \
   103	        do                                                                                             \
   104	        {                                                                                              \
   105	                if ((period) <= 0)                                                                         \
   106	                        ereport(ERROR,                                                                         \
   107	                                        (errcode(ERRCODE_INVALID_PARAMETER_VALUE),                                     \
   108	                                         errmsg("period must be greater than 0")));                                    \
   109	                /* shift = shift % period, but use TMODULO */                                              \
   110	                TMODULO(shift, result, period);                                                            \
   111	                                                                                                   \
   112	                if (((shift) > 0 && (timestamp) < DT_NOBEGIN + (shift)) ||                                 \
   113	                        ((shift) < 0 && (timestamp) > DT_NOEND + (shift)))                                     \
   114	                        ereport(ERROR,                                                                         \
   115	                                        (errcode(ERRCODE_NUMERIC_VALUE_OUT_OF_RANGE),                                  \
   116	                                         errmsg("timestamp out of range")));                                           \
   117	                (timestamp) -= (shift);                                                                    \
   118	                                                                                                   \
   119	                /* result = (timestamp / period) * period */                                               \
   120	                TMODULO(timestamp, result, period);                                                        \
   121	                if ((timestamp) < 0)                                                                       \
   122	                {                                                                                          \
   123	                        /*                                                                                     \
   124	                         * need to subtract another period if remainder < 0 this only happens                  \
   125	                         * if timestamp is negative to begin with and there is a remainder                     \
   126	                         * after division. Need to subtract another period since division                      \
   127	                         * truncates toward 0 in C99.                                                          \
   128	                         */                                                                                    \
   129	                        (result) = ((result) * (period)) - (period);                                           \
   130	                }                                                                                          \
   131	                else                                                                                       \
   132	                        (result) *= (period);                                                                  \
   133	                                                                                                   \
   134	                (result) += (shift);                                                                       \
   135	        } while (0)
   136	
   137	static void
   138	validate_month_bucket(Interval *interval)
   139	{
   140	        /*
   141	         * Bucketing by a month and non-month cannot be mixed.
   142	         */
   143	        Assert(interval->month);
   144	
   145	        if (interval->day || interval->time)
   146	        {
   147	                ereport(ERROR,
   148	                                (errcode(ERRCODE_FEATURE_NOT_SUPPORTED),
   149	                                 errmsg("month intervals cannot have day or time component")));
   150	        }
   151	}
   152	
   153	/*
   154	 * To bucket by month we get the year and month of a date and convert
   155	 * that to the nth month since origin. This allows us to treat month
   156	 * bucketing similar to int bucketing. During this process we ignore
   157	 * the day component and therefore only support bucketing by full months.
   158	 */
   159	static DateADT
   160	bucket_month(int32 period, DateADT date, DateADT origin)
   161	{
   162	        int32 year, month, day;
   163	        int32 result;
   164	
   165	        j2date(date + POSTGRES_EPOCH_JDATE, &year, &month, &day);
   166	        int32 timestamp = (year * 12) + month - 1;
   167	
   168	        j2date(origin + POSTGRES_EPOCH_JDATE, &year, &month, &day);
   169	        int32 offset = (year * 12) + month - 1;
   170	
   171	        TIME_BUCKET(period, timestamp, offset, PG_INT32_MIN, PG_INT32_MAX, result);
   172	
   173	        year = result / 12;
   174	        month = result % 12;
   175	        day = 1;
   176	
   177	        return date2j(year, month + 1, day) - POSTGRES_EPOCH_JDATE;
   178	}
   179	
   180	/* Returns the period in the same representation as Postgres Timestamps.
   181	 * Note that this is not our internal representation (microseconds).
   182	 * Always returns an exact value.*/
   183	static inline int64
   184	get_interval_period_timestamp_units(Interval *interval)
   185	{
   186	        if (interval->month != 0)
   187	        {
   188	                ereport(ERROR,
   189	                                (errcode(ERRCODE_FEATURE_NOT_SUPPORTED),
   190	                                 errmsg("interval defined in terms of month, year, century etc. not supported")));
   191	        }
   192	        return interval->time + (interval->day * USECS_PER_DAY);
   193	}

   197	TSDLLEXPORT Datum
   198	ts_timestamp_bucket(PG_FUNCTION_ARGS)
   199	{
   200	        Interval *interval = PG_GETARG_INTERVAL_P(0);
   201	        Timestamp timestamp = PG_GETARG_TIMESTAMP(1);
   202	
   203	        /*
   204	         * USE NARGS and not IS_NULL to differentiate a NULL argument from a call
   205	         * with 2 parameters
   206	         */
   207	        Timestamp origin = (PG_NARGS() > 2 ? PG_GETARG_TIMESTAMP(2) : DEFAULT_ORIGIN);
   208	        Timestamp result;
   209	
   210	        if (TIMESTAMP_NOT_FINITE(timestamp))
   211	                PG_RETURN_TIMESTAMP(timestamp);
   212	
   213	        if (interval->month)
   214	        {
   215	                DateADT origin_date = 0;
   216	                validate_month_bucket(interval);
   217	
   218	                DateADT date = DatumGetDateADT(DirectFunctionCall1(timestamp_date, PG_GETARG_DATUM(1)));
   219	                if (origin != DEFAULT_ORIGIN)
   220	                        origin_date =
   221	                                DatumGetDateADT(DirectFunctionCall1(timestamp_date, TimestampGetDatum(origin)));
   222	
   223	                date = bucket_month(interval->month, date, origin_date);
   224	
   225	                PG_RETURN_DATUM(DirectFunctionCall1(date_timestamp, DateADTGetDatum(date)));
   226	        }
   227	        else
   228	        {
   229	                int64 period = get_interval_period_timestamp_units(interval);
   230	
   231	                TIME_BUCKET_TS(period, timestamp, result, origin);
   232	
   233	                PG_RETURN_TIMESTAMP(result);
   234	        }
   235	}

   242	        Datum period = PG_GETARG_DATUM(0);

   319	TS_FUNCTION_INFO_V1(ts_timestamptz_timezone_bucket);
   320	
   321	/*
   322	 * time_bucket(bucket_width INTERVAL, ts TIMESTAMPTZ, timezone TEXT, origin TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT
   323	 * NULL, "offset" INTERVAL DEFAULT NULL) RETURNS TIMESTAMPTZ
   324	 */
   325	TSDLLEXPORT Datum
   326	ts_timestamptz_timezone_bucket(PG_FUNCTION_ARGS)
   327	{
   328	        Datum period = PG_GETARG_DATUM(0);
   329	        Datum timestamp = PG_GETARG_DATUM(1);
   330	        Datum tzname = PG_GETARG_DATUM(2);
   331	
   332	        /*
   333	         * When called from SQL we will always have 5 args because default values
   334	         * will be filled in for missing arguments. When called from C with
   335	         * DirectFunctionCall number of arguments might be less than 5.
   336	         */
   337	        bool have_origin = PG_NARGS() > 3 && !PG_ARGISNULL(3);
   338	        bool have_offset = PG_NARGS() > 4 && !PG_ARGISNULL(4);
   339	
   340	        /*
   341	         * We need to check for NULL arguments here because the function cannot be
   342	         * defined STRICT due to the optional arguments.
   343	         */
   344	        if (PG_ARGISNULL(0) || PG_ARGISNULL(1) || PG_ARGISNULL(2))
   345	                PG_RETURN_NULL();
   346	
   347	        /* Convert to local timestamp according to timezone */
   348	        timestamp = DirectFunctionCall2(timestamptz_zone, tzname, timestamp);
   349	        if (have_offset)
   350	        {
   351	                /* Apply offset. */
   352	                timestamp = DirectFunctionCall2(timestamp_mi_interval, timestamp, PG_GETARG_DATUM(4));
   353	        }
   354	
   355	        if (have_origin)
   356	        {
   357	                Datum origin = DirectFunctionCall2(timestamptz_zone, tzname, PG_GETARG_DATUM(3));
   358	                timestamp = DirectFunctionCall3(ts_timestamp_bucket, period, timestamp, origin);
   359	        }
   360	        else
   361	        {
   362	                timestamp = DirectFunctionCall2(ts_timestamp_bucket, period, timestamp);
   363	        }
   364	
   365	        if (have_offset)
   366	        {
   367	                /* Remove offset. */
   368	                timestamp = DirectFunctionCall2(timestamp_pl_interval, timestamp, PG_GETARG_DATUM(4));
   369	        }
   370	
   371	        /* Convert back to timezone */
   372	        timestamp = DirectFunctionCall2(timestamp_zone, tzname, timestamp);
   373	
   374	        PG_RETURN_DATUM(timestamp);
   375	}
   376	
   377	static inline void
   378	check_period_is_daily(int64 period)
   379	{
   380	        int64 day = USECS_PER_DAY;
   381	
   382	        if (period < day)
   383	        {
   384	                ereport(ERROR,
   385	                                (errcode(ERRCODE_FEATURE_NOT_SUPPORTED),
   386	                                 errmsg("interval must not have sub-day precision")));
   387	        }
   388	        if (period % day != 0)
   389	        {
   390	                ereport(ERROR,
   391	                                (errcode(ERRCODE_FEATURE_NOT_SUPPORTED),
   392	                                 errmsg("interval must be a multiple of a day")));
   393	        }
   394	}

   158	/* API to update materializations from refresh code */
   159	void
   160	continuous_agg_update_materialization(Hypertable *mat_ht, const ContinuousAgg *cagg,
   161	                                                                          SchemaAndName partial_view,
   162	                                                                          SchemaAndName materialization_table,
   163	                                                                          const NameData *time_column_name,
   164	                                                                          InternalTimeRange materialization_range, int32 chunk_id)
   165	{
   166	        MaterializationContext context = {
   167	                .mat_ht = mat_ht,
   168	                .cagg = cagg,
   169	                .partial_view = partial_view,
   170	                .materialization_table = materialization_table,
   171	                .time_column_name = (NameData *) time_column_name,
   172	                .materialization_range = internal_time_range_to_time_range(materialization_range),
   173	                .internal_materialization_range = materialization_range,
   174	                /*
   175	                 * chunk_id is valid if the materializaion update should be done only on the given chunk.
   176	                 * This is used currently for refresh on chunk drop only. In other cases, manual
   177	                 * call to refresh_continuous_aggregate or call from a refresh policy, chunk_id is
   178	                 * not provided, i.e., invalid. Also the chunk_id is used only on the old format.
   179	                 */
   180	                .chunk_condition =
   181	                        chunk_id != INVALID_CHUNK_ID && !ContinuousAggIsFinalized(cagg) ?
   182	                                psprintf(" AND %s = %d", CONTINUOUS_AGG_CHUNK_ID_COL_NAME, chunk_id) :
   183	                                "",
   184	        };
   185	
   186	        /* Lock down search_path */
   187	        int save_nestlevel = NewGUCNestLevel();
   188	        RestrictSearchPath();
   189	
   190	        /* pin the start of new_materialization to the end of new_materialization,
   191	         * we are not allowed to materialize beyond that point
   192	         */
   193	        if (materialization_range.start > materialization_range.end)
   194	                materialization_range.start = materialization_range.end;
   195	
   196	        /* Then insert the materializations */
   197	        context.materialization_range = internal_time_range_to_time_range(materialization_range);
   198	        execute_materializations(&context);
   199	
   200	        /* Restore search_path */
   201	        AtEOXact_GUC(false, save_nestlevel);
   202	}
   203	
   204	static Datum
   205	time_range_internal_to_min_time_value(Oid type)
   206	{
   207	        switch (type)
   208	        {
   209	                case TIMESTAMPOID:
   210	                        return TimestampGetDatum(DT_NOBEGIN);
   211	                case TIMESTAMPTZOID:
   212	                        return TimestampTzGetDatum(DT_NOBEGIN);
   213	                case DATEOID:
   214	                        return DateADTGetDatum(DATEVAL_NOBEGIN);
   215	                default:
   216	                        return ts_internal_to_time_value(PG_INT64_MIN, type);
   217	        }
   218	}
   219	
   220	static Datum
   221	time_range_internal_to_max_time_value(Oid type)
   222	{
   223	        switch (type)
   224	        {
   225	                case TIMESTAMPOID:
   226	                        return TimestampGetDatum(DT_NOEND);
   227	                case TIMESTAMPTZOID:
   228	                        return TimestampTzGetDatum(DT_NOEND);
   229	                case DATEOID:
   230	                        return DateADTGetDatum(DATEVAL_NOEND);
   231	                        break;
   232	                default:
   233	                        return ts_internal_to_time_value(PG_INT64_MAX, type);
   234	        }
   235	}
   236	
   237	static Datum
   238	internal_to_time_value_or_infinite(int64 internal, Oid time_type, bool *is_infinite_out)
   239	{
   240	        /* MIN and MAX can occur due to NULL thresholds, or due to a lack of invalidations. Since our
   241	         * regular conversion function errors in those cases, and we want to use those as markers for an
   242	         * open threshold in one direction, we special case this here*/
   243	        if (internal == PG_INT64_MIN)
   244	        {
   245	                if (is_infinite_out != NULL)
   246	                        *is_infinite_out = true;
   247	                return time_range_internal_to_min_time_value(time_type);
   248	        }
   249	        else if (internal == PG_INT64_MAX)
   250	        {
   251	                if (is_infinite_out != NULL)
   252	                        *is_infinite_out = true;
   253	                return time_range_internal_to_max_time_value(time_type);
   254	        }
   255	        else
   256	        {
   257	                if (is_infinite_out != NULL)
   258	                        *is_infinite_out = false;
   259	                return ts_internal_to_time_value(internal, time_type);
   260	        }
   261	}
   262	
   263	static TimeRange
   264	internal_time_range_to_time_range(InternalTimeRange internal)
   265	{
   266	        TimeRange range;
   267	        range.type = internal.type;
   268	
   269	        range.start = internal_to_time_value_or_infinite(internal.start, internal.type, NULL);
   270	        range.end = internal_to_time_value_or_infinite(internal.end, internal.type, NULL);
   271	
   272	        return range;
   273	}
   274	
   275	static List *
   276	cagg_find_aggref_and_var_cols(ContinuousAgg *cagg, Hypertable *mat_ht)
   277	{
   278	        List *retlist = NIL;
   279	        ListCell *lc;
   280	        Query *cagg_view_query = ts_continuous_agg_get_query(cagg);
   281	
   282	        foreach (lc, cagg_view_query->targetList)
   283	        {
   284	                TargetEntry *tle = castNode(TargetEntry, lfirst(lc));
   285	
   286	                if (!tle->resjunk && (tle->ressortgroupref == 0 ||
   287	                                                          get_sortgroupref_clause_noerr(tle->ressortgroupref,
   288	                                                                                                                        cagg_view_query->groupClause) == NULL))
   289	                        retlist = lappend(retlist, get_attname(mat_ht->main_table_relid, tle->resno, false));
   290	        }
   291	
   292	        return retlist;
   293	}
   294	
   295	static char *
   296	build_merge_insert_columns(List *strings, const char *separator, const char *prefix)
   297	{
   298	        StringInfo ret = makeStringInfo();
   299	
   300	        Assert(strings != NIL);
   301	
   302	        ListCell *lc;
   303	        foreach (lc, strings)
   304	        {
   305	                char *grpcol = (char *) lfirst(lc);
   306	                if (ret->len > 0)
   307	                        appendStringInfoString(ret, separator);
   308	
   309	                if (prefix)
   310	                        appendStringInfoString(ret, prefix);
   311	                appendStringInfoString(ret, quote_identifier(grpcol));
   312	        }
   313	
   314	        elog(DEBUG2, "%s: %s", __func__, ret->data);
   315	        return ret->data;
   316	}
   317	
   318	static char *
   319	build_merge_join_clause(List *column_names)
   320	{
   321	        StringInfo ret = makeStringInfo();
   322	
   323	        Assert(column_names != NIL);
   324	
   325	        ListCell *lc;
   326	        foreach (lc, column_names)
   327	        {
   328	                char *column = (char *) lfirst(lc);
   329	
   330	                if (ret->len > 0)
   331	                        appendStringInfoString(ret, " AND ");
   332	
   333	                appendStringInfoString(ret, "P.");
   334	                appendStringInfoString(ret, quote_identifier(column));
   335	                appendStringInfoString(ret, " IS NOT DISTINCT FROM M.");
   336	                appendStringInfoString(ret, quote_identifier(column));
   337	        }
   338	
   339	        elog(DEBUG2, "%s: %s", __func__, ret->data);
   340	        return ret->data;
   341	}
   342	
   343	static char *
   344	build_merge_update_clause(List *column_names)
   345	{
   346	        StringInfo ret = makeStringInfo();
   347	
   348	        Assert(column_names != NIL);
   349	
   350	        ListCell *lc;
   351	        foreach (lc, column_names)
   352	        {
   353	                char *column = (char *) lfirst(lc);
   354	
   355	                if (ret->len > 0)
   356	                        appendStringInfoString(ret, ", ");
   357	
   358	                appendStringInfoString(ret, quote_identifier(column));
   359	                appendStringInfoString(ret, " = P.");
   360	                appendStringInfoString(ret, quote_identifier(column));
   361	        }
   362	
   363	        elog(DEBUG2, "%s: %s", __func__, ret->data);
   364	        return ret->data;
   365	}
   366	
   367	/* Create INSERT statement */
   368	static char *
   369	create_materialization_insert_statement(MaterializationContext *context)
   370	{
   371	        StringInfoData query;
   372	        initStringInfo(&query);
   373	        appendStringInfo(&query,
   374	                                         "INSERT INTO %s.%s SELECT * FROM %s.%s AS I "
   375	                                         "WHERE I.%s >= $1 AND I.%s < $2 %s;",
   376	                                         quote_identifier(NameStr(*context->materialization_table.schema)),
   377	                                         quote_identifier(NameStr(*context->materialization_table.name)),
   378	                                         quote_identifier(NameStr(*context->partial_view.schema)),
   379	                                         quote_identifier(NameStr(*context->partial_view.name)),
   380	                                         quote_identifier(NameStr(*context->time_column_name)),
   381	                                         quote_identifier(NameStr(*context->time_column_name)),
   382	                                         context->chunk_condition);
   383	        return query.data;
   384	}
   385	
   386	/* Create DELETE statement */
   387	static char *
   388	create_materialization_delete_statement(MaterializationContext *context)
   389	{
   390	        StringInfoData query;
   391	        initStringInfo(&query);
   392	        appendStringInfo(&query,
   393	                                         "DELETE FROM %s.%s AS D "
   394	                                         "WHERE D.%s >= $1 AND D.%s < $2 %s;",
   395	                                         quote_identifier(NameStr(*context->materialization_table.schema)),
   396	                                         quote_identifier(NameStr(*context->materialization_table.name)),
   397	                                         quote_identifier(NameStr(*context->time_column_name)),
   398	                                         quote_identifier(NameStr(*context->time_column_name)),
   399	                                         context->chunk_condition);
   400	        return query.data;
   401	}
   402	
   403	/* Create SELECT EXISTS statement */
   404	static char *
   405	create_materialization_exists_statement(MaterializationContext *context)
   406	{
   407	        StringInfoData query;
   408	        initStringInfo(&query);
   409	        appendStringInfo(&query,
   410	                                         "SELECT 1 FROM %s.%s AS M "
   411	                                         "WHERE M.%s >= $1 AND M.%s < $2 "
   412	                                         "LIMIT 1;",
   413	                                         quote_identifier(NameStr(*context->materialization_table.schema)),
   414	                                         quote_identifier(NameStr(*context->materialization_table.name)),
   415	                                         quote_identifier(NameStr(*context->time_column_name)),
   416	                                         quote_identifier(NameStr(*context->time_column_name)));
   417	        return query.data;
   418	}
   419	
   420	/* Create MERGE statement */
   421	static char *
   422	create_materialization_merge_statement(MaterializationContext *context)
   423	{
   424	        List *grp_colnames = cagg_find_groupingcols((ContinuousAgg *) context->cagg, context->mat_ht);
   425	        List *agg_colnames =
   426	                cagg_find_aggref_and_var_cols((ContinuousAgg *) context->cagg, context->mat_ht);
   427	        List *all_columns = NIL;
   428	
   429	        /* Concat both lists into a single one*/
   430	        all_columns = list_concat(all_columns, grp_colnames);
   431	        all_columns = list_concat(all_columns, agg_colnames);
   432	
   433	        StringInfoData merge_update;
   434	        initStringInfo(&merge_update);
   435	        char *merge_update_clause = build_merge_update_clause(all_columns);
   436	
   437	        /* It make no sense but is possible to create a cagg only with time bucket (without
   438	         * aggregate functions) */
   439	        if (merge_update_clause != NULL)
   440	        {
   441	                appendStringInfo(&merge_update,
   442	                                                 "  WHEN MATCHED AND ROW(M.*) IS DISTINCT FROM ROW(P.*) THEN "
   443	                                                 "    UPDATE SET %s ",
   444	                                                 merge_update_clause);
   445	        }
   446	
   447	        StringInfoData query;
   448	        initStringInfo(&query);
   449	
   450	        /* MERGE statement to UPDATE affected buckets and INSERT new ones */
   451	        appendStringInfo(&query,
   452	                                         "WITH partial AS ( "
   453	                                         "  SELECT * "
   454	                                         "  FROM %s.%s "
   455	                                         "  WHERE %s >= $1 AND %s < $2 "
   456	                                         ") "
   457	                                         "MERGE INTO %s.%s M "
   458	                                         "USING partial P ON %s AND M.%s >= $1 AND M.%s < $2 "
   459	                                         "  %s " /* UPDATE */
   460	                                         "  WHEN NOT MATCHED THEN "
   461	                                         "    INSERT (%s) VALUES (%s) ",
   462	
   463	                                         /* partial VIEW */
   464	                                         quote_identifier(NameStr(*context->partial_view.schema)),
   465	                                         quote_identifier(NameStr(*context->partial_view.name)),
   466	
   467	                                         /* partial WHERE */
   468	                                         quote_identifier(NameStr(*context->time_column_name)),
   469	                                         quote_identi<response clipped><NOTE>To save on context only part of this file has been shown to you. """
Script to reproduce the continuous aggregate timezone issue.
This script creates a PostgreSQL database and attempts to reproduce the bug.
"""

import subprocess
import time
import psycopg2
import sys

# PostgreSQL connection parameters
DB_HOST = "localhost"
DB_PORT = "5432"
DB_NAME = "test_db"
DB_USER = "postgres"
DB_PASSWORD = "password"

def run_sql(sql):
    """Execute SQL command and return result"""
    try:
        conn = psycopg2.connect(
            host=DB_HOST,
            port=DB_PORT,
            database=DB_NAME,
            user=DB_USER,
            password=DB_PASSWORD
        )
        conn.autocommit = True
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        cursor.execute(sql)
        
        if cursor.description:
            result = cursor.fetchall()
        else:
            result = None
            
        conn.close()
        return result
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Error executing SQL: {e}")
        return None

def create_test_environment():
    """Create the test environment as described in the PR"""
    print("Creating test environment...")
    
    # Create the hypertable
    run_sql("""
    CREATE TABLE metrics (
        sensor_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
        value DOUBLE PRECISION NOT NULL,
        timestamp TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL
    );
    """)
    
    run_sql("SELECT create_hypertable('"'"'metrics'"'"', '"'"'timestamp'"'"');")
    
    # Insert data
    run_sql("""
    INSERT INTO metrics
    SELECT
        s.sensor_id,
        random()*50 + 10,
        timestamp
    FROM
        generate_series(DATE (now() - interval '"'"'6 month'"'"'), (now() - interval '"'"'5 day'"'"'), INTERVAL '"'"'1 hours'"'"') AS timestamp
            CROSS JOIN (SELECT generate_series(1, 200) as sensor_id) as s;
    """)
    
    # Create continuous aggregate with timezone
    run_sql("""
    CREATE MATERIALIZED VIEW datalake_hourly
    WITH (timescaledb.continuous, timescaledb.materialized_only = true) AS
                SELECT
                    time_bucket(INTERVAL '"'"'1 hour'"'"', metrics.timestamp, '"'"'Asia/Dubai'"'"') AS bucket,
                    sensor_id,
                    count(*) as count_items
                FROM metrics
                GROUP BY bucket, sensor_id;
    """)
    
    # Add continuous aggregate policy
    run_sql("""
    SELECT add_continuous_aggregate_policy(
            '"'"'datalake_hourly'"'"',
            start_offset => INTERVAL '"'"'3 months'"'"',
            end_offset => Null,
            schedule_interval => INTERVAL '"'"'15 seconds'"'"'
    );
    """)
    
    # Insert more data
    run_sql("""
    INSERT INTO metrics
    SELECT
        s.sensor_id,
        random()*50 + 10,
        timestamp
    FROM
        generate_series((now() - interval '"'"'5 day'"'"'), now(), INTERVAL '"'"'1 hour'"'"') AS timestamp
            CROSS JOIN (SELECT generate_series(1, 200) as sensor_id) as s;
    """)

def check_job_status():
    """Check the status of the continuous aggregate job"""
    print("\nChecking job status...")
    
    result = run_sql("""
    SELECT 
            timescaledb_information.jobs.job_id,
            timescaledb_information.jobs.application_name,
            timescaledb_information.jobs.initial_start,
            timescaledb_information.jobs.next_start,
            timescaledb_information.jobs.config,
            timescaledb_information.jobs.schedule_interval,
            timescaledb_information.jobs.max_runtime ,
            timescaledb_information.jobs.max_retries  ,   
            timescaledb_information.jobs.retry_period ,  
            timescaledb_information.jobs.scheduled ,
            timescaledb_information.jobs.fixed_schedule , 
            timescaledb_information.jobs.hypertable_name , 
            timescaledb_information.continuous_aggregates.view_name ,
            last_run_started_at ,
           job_status,
           last_run_status,
           last_successful_finish ,
           total_runs,
           total_failures ,
           total_successes 
    FROM timescaledb_information.jobs
    left join timescaledb_information.job_stats on timescaledb_information.jobs.job_id  =  timescaledb_information.job_stats.job_id 
    left join timescaledb_information.continuous_aggregates on timescaledb_information.continuous_aggregates.materialization_hypertable_name  =  timescaledb_information.jobs.hypertable_name
    order by job_id;
    """)
    
    if result:
        print("Job status:")
        for row in result:
            print(f"  Job ID: {row[0]}, Status: {row[14]}, Last Run: {row[15]}")
    
    # Check continuous aggregate data
    result = run_sql("SELECT count(*) FROM datalake_hourly;")
    if result:
        print(f"\nRows in continuous aggregate: {result[0][0]}")
    
    # Check if new data is being materialized
    result = run_sql("""
    SELECT max(bucket) FROM datalake_hourly;
    """)
    if result:
        print(f"Latest bucket in continuous aggregate: {result[0][0]}")
        
    result = run_sql("""
    SELECT max(timestamp) FROM metrics;
    """)
    if result:
        print(f"Latest timestamp in raw data: {result[0][0]}")

def main():
    print("Starting reproduction of continuous aggregate timezone issue...")
    
    # Create test environment
    create_test_environment()
    
    # Wait for the job to run
    print("\nWaiting 30 seconds for the continuous aggregate job to run...")
    time.sleep(30)
    
    # Check job status
    check_job_status()
    
    print("\nTest completed.")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    if len(sys.argv) > 1 and sys.argv[1] == "--setup":
        # Just setup the database
        create_test_environment()
        print("Database setup complete.")
    else:
        main()'

			policy_refresh_cagg_check_for_overlaps(cagg, job->fd.config, job->fd.id);
		switch (res)
		{
			case POLICY_REFRESH_OFFSET_OVERLAP_NONE:
				break;
			case POLICY_REFRESH_OFFSET_OVERLAP_EQUAL:

    42	RETURNS void AS '@MODULE_PATHNAME@', 'ts_policy_process_hyper_inval_check'
